concreteSeries struct {\n   368→\tlabels     labels.Labels\n   369→\tfloats     []prompb.Sample\n   370→\thistograms []prompb.Histogram\n   371→}\n   372→\n   373→func (c *concreteSeries) Labels() labels.Labels {\n   374→\treturn c.labels.Copy()\n   375→}\n   376→\n   377→func (c *concreteSeries) Iterator(it chunkenc.Iterator) chunkenc.Iterator {\n   378→\tif csi, ok := it.(*concreteSeriesIterator); ok {\n   379→\t\tcsi.reset(c)\n   380→\t\treturn csi\n   381→\t}\n   382→\treturn newConcreteSeriesIterator(c)\n   383→}\n   384→\n   385→// concreteSeriesIterator implements storage.SeriesIterator.\n   386→type concreteSeriesIterator struct {\n   387→\tfloatsCur     int\n   388→\thistogramsCur int\n   389→\tcurValType    chunkenc.ValueType\n   390→\tseries        *concreteSeries\n   391→\terr           error\n   392→\n   393→\t// These are pre-filled with the current model histogram if curValType\n   394→\t// is ValHistogram or ValFloatHistogram, respectively.\n   395→\tcurH  *histogram.Histogram\n   396→\tcurFH *histogram.FloatHistogram\n   397→}\n   398→\n   399→func newConcreteSeriesIterator(series *concreteSeries) chunkenc.Iterator {\n   400→\treturn &concreteSeriesIterator{\n   401→\t\tfloatsCur:     -1,\n   402→\t\thistogramsCur: -1,\n   403→\t\tcurValType:    chunkenc.ValNone,\n   404→\t\tseries:        series,\n   405→\t}\n   406→}\n   407→\n   408→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) reset(series *concreteSeries) {\n   409→\tc.floatsCur = -1\n   410→\tc.histogramsCur = -1\n   411→\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   412→\tc.series = series\n   413→\tc.err = nil\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→// Seek implements storage.SeriesIterator.\n   417→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) Seek(t int64) chunkenc.ValueType {\n   418→\tif c.err != nil {\n   419→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   420→\t}\n   421→\tif c.floatsCur == -1 {\n   422→\t\tc.floatsCur = 0\n   423→\t}\n   424→\tif c.histogramsCur == -1 {\n   425→\t\tc.histogramsCur = 0\n   426→\t}\n   427→\tif c.floatsCur >= len(c.series.floats) && c.histogramsCur >= len(c.series.histograms) {\n   428→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   429→\t}\n   430→\n   431→\t// No-op check.\n   432→\tif (c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloat && c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp >= t) ||\n   433→\t\t((c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram || c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram) && c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp >= t) {\n   434→\t\treturn c.curValType\n   435→\t}\n   436→\n   437→\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   438→\n   439→\t// Binary search between current position and end for both float and histograms samples.\n   440→\tc.floatsCur += sort.Search(len(c.series.floats)-c.floatsCur, func(n int) bool {\n   441→\t\treturn c.series.floats[n+c.floatsCur].Timestamp >= t\n   442→\t})\n   443→\tc.histogramsCur += sort.Search(len(c.series.histograms)-c.histogramsCur, func(n int) bool {\n   444→\t\treturn c.series.histograms[n+c.histogramsCur].Timestamp >= t\n   445→\t})\n   446→\tswitch {\n   447→\tcase c.floatsCur < len(c.series.floats) && c.histogramsCur < len(c.series.histograms):\n   448→\t\t// If float samples and histogram samples have overlapping timestamps prefer the float samples.\n   449→\t\tif c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp <= c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp {\n   450→\t\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n   451→\t\t} else {\n   452→\t\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n   453→\t\t}\n   454→\t\t// When the timestamps do not overlap the cursor for the non-selected sample type has advanced too\n   455→\t\t// far; we decrement it back down here.\n   456→\t\tif c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp != c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp {\n   457→\t\t\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloat {\n   458→\t\t\t\tc.histogramsCur--\n   459→\t\t\t} else {\n   460→\t\t\t\tc.floatsCur--\n   461→\t\t\t}\n   462→\t\t}\n   463→\tcase c.floatsCur < len(c.series.floats):\n   464→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n   465→\tcase c.histogramsCur < len(c.series.histograms):\n   466→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n   467→\t}\n   468→\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram {\n   469→\t\tc.setCurrentHistogram()\n   470→\t}\n   471→\tif c.err != nil {\n   472→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   473→\t}\n   474→\treturn c.curValType\n   475→}\n   476→\n   477→// setCurrentHistogram pre-fills either the curH or the curFH field with a\n   478→// converted model histogram and sets c.curValType accordingly. It validates the\n   479→// histogram and sets c.err accordingly. This all has to be done in Seek() and\n   480→// Next() already so that we know if the histogram we got from the remote-read\n   481→// source is valid or not before we allow the AtHistogram()/AtFloatHistogram()\n   482→// call.\n   483→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) setCurrentHistogram() {\n   484→\tpbH := c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur]\n   485→\n   486→\t// Basic schema check first.\n   487→\tschema := pbH.Schema\n   488→\tif !histogram.IsKnownSchema(schema) {\n   489→\t\tc.err = histogram.UnknownSchemaError(schema)\n   490→\t\treturn\n   491→\t}\n   492→\n   493→\tif pbH.IsFloatHistogram() {\n   494→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram\n   495→\t\tmFH := pbH.ToFloatHistogram()\n   496→\t\tif mFH.Schema > histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax && mFH.Schema <= histogram.ExponentialSchemaMaxReserved {\n   497→\t\t\t// This is a very slow path, but it should only happen if the\n   498→\t\t\t// sample is from a newer Prometheus version that supports higher\n   499→\t\t\t// resolution.\n   500→\t\t\tif err := mFH.ReduceResolution(histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax); err != nil {\n   501→\t\t\t\tc.err = err\n   502→\t\t\t\treturn\n   503→\t\t\t}\n   504→\t\t}\n   505→\t\tif err := mFH.Validate(); err != nil {\n   506→\t\t\tc.err = err\n   507→\t\t\treturn\n   508→\t\t}\n   509→\t\tc.curFH = mFH\n   510→\t\treturn\n   511→\t}\n   512→\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n   513→\tmH := pbH.ToIntHistogram()\n   514→\tif mH.Schema > histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax && mH.Schema <= histogram.ExponentialSchemaMaxReserved {\n   515→\t\t// This is a very slow path, but it should only happen if the\n   516→\t\t// sample is from a newer Prometheus version that supports higher\n   517→\t\t// resolution.\n   518→\t\tif err := mH.ReduceResolution(histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax); err != nil {\n   519→\t\t\tc.err = err\n   520→\t\t\treturn\n   521→\t\t}\n   522→\t}\n   523→\tif err := mH.Validate(); err != nil {\n   524→\t\tc.err = err\n   525→\t\treturn\n   526→\t}\n   527→\tc.curH = mH\n   528→}\n   529→\n   530→// At implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   531→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) At() (t int64, v float64) {\n   532→\tif c.curValType != chunkenc.ValFloat {\n   533→\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on a float sample\")\n   534→\t}\n   535→\ts := c.series.floats[c.floatsCur]\n   536→\treturn s.Timestamp, s.Value\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→// AtHistogram implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   540→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtHistogram(*histogram.Histogram) (int64, *histogram.Histogram) {\n   541→\tif c.curValType != chunkenc.ValHistogram {\n   542→\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on an integer histogram sample\")\n   543→\t}\n   544→\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curH\n   545→}\n   546→\n   547→// AtFloatHistogram implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   548→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtFloatHistogram(*histogram.FloatHistogram) (int64, *histogram.FloatHistogram) {\n   549→\tswitch c.curValType {\n   550→\tcase chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram:\n   551→\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curFH\n   552→\tcase chunkenc.ValHistogram:\n   553→\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curH.ToFloat(nil)\n   554→\tdefault:\n   555→\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on a histogram sample\")\n   556→\t}\n   557→}\n   558→\n   559→// AtT implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   560→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtT() int64 {\n   561→\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram || c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram {\n   562→\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp\n   563→\t}\n   564→\treturn c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→// TODO(krajorama): implement AtST. Maybe. concreteSeriesIterator is used\n   568→// for turning query results into an iterable, but query results do not have ST.\n   569→func (*concreteSeriesIterator) AtST() int64 {\n   570→\treturn 0\n   571→}\n   572→\n   573→const noTS = int64(math.MaxInt64)\n   574→\n   575→// Next implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   576→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) Next() chunkenc.ValueType {\n   577→\tif c.err != nil {\n   578→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   579→\t}\n   580→\tpeekFloatTS := noTS\n   581→\tif c.floatsCur+1 < len(c.series.floats) {\n   582→\t\tpeekFloatTS = c.series.floats[c.floatsCur+1].Timestamp\n   583→\t}\n   584→\tpeekHistTS := noTS\n   585→\tif c.histogramsCur+1 < len(c.series.histograms) {\n   586→\t\tpeekHistTS = c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur+1].Timestamp\n   587→\t}\n   588→\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   589→\tswitch {\n   590→\tcase peekFloatTS < peekHistTS:\n   591→\t\tc.floatsCur++\n   592→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n   593→\tcase peekHistTS < peekFloatTS:\n   594→\t\tc.histogramsCur++\n   595→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n   596→\tcase peekFloatTS == noTS && peekHistTS == noTS:\n   597→\t\t// This only happens when the iterator is exhausted; we set the cursors off the end to prevent\n   598→\t\t// Seek() from returning anything afterwards.\n   599→\t\tc.floatsCur = len(c.series.floats)\n   600→\t\tc.histogramsCur = len(c.series.histograms)\n   601→\tdefault:\n   602→\t\t// Prefer float samples to histogram samples if there's a conflict. We advance the cursor for histograms\n   603→\t\t// anyway otherwise the histogram sample will get selected on the next call to Next().\n   604→\t\tc.floatsCur++\n   605→\t\tc.histogramsCur++\n   606→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n   607→\t}\n   608→\n   609→\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram {\n   610→\t\tc.setCurrentHistogram()\n   611→\t}\n   612→\tif c.err != nil {\n   613→\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   614→\t}\n   615→\treturn c.curValType\n   616→}\n   617→\n   618→// Err implements chunkenc.Iterator.\n   619→func (c *concreteSeriesIterator) Err() error {\n   620→\treturn c.err\n   621→}\n   622→\n   623→// chunkedSeriesSet implements storage.SeriesSet.\n   624→type chunkedSeriesSet struct {\n   625→\tchunkedReader *ChunkedReader\n   626→\trespBody      io.ReadCloser\n   627→\tmint, maxt    int64\n   628→\tcancel        func(error)\n   629→\n   630→\tcurrent   storage.Series\n   631→\terr       error\n   632→\texhausted bool\n   633→}\n   634→\n   635→func NewChunkedSeriesSet(chunkedReader *ChunkedReader, respBody io.ReadCloser, mint, maxt int64, cancel func(error)) storage.SeriesSet {\n   636→\treturn &chunkedSeriesSet{\n   637→\t\tchunkedReader: chunkedReader,\n   638→\t\trespBody:      respBody,\n   639→\t\tmint:          mint,\n   640→\t\tmaxt:          maxt,\n   641→\t\tcancel:        cancel,\n   642→\t}\n   643→}\n   644→\n   645→// Next return true if there is a next series and false otherwise. It will\n   646→// block until the next series is available.\n   647→func (s *chunkedSeriesSet) Next() bool {\n   648→\tif s.exhausted {\n   649→\t\t// Don't try to read the next series again.\n   650→\t\t// This prevents errors like \"http: read on closed response body\" if Next() is called after it has already returned false.\n   651→\t\treturn false\n   652→\t}\n   653→\n   654→\tres := &prompb.ChunkedReadResponse{}\n   655→\n   656→\terr := s.chunkedReader.NextProto(res)\n   657→\tif err != nil {\n   658→\t\tif !errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n   659→\t\t\ts.err = err\n   660→\t\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, s.respBody)\n   661→\t\t}\n   662→\n   663→\t\t_ = s.respBody.Close()\n   664→\t\ts.cancel(err)\n   665→\t\ts.exhausted = true\n   666→\n   667→\t\treturn false\n   668→\t}\n   669→\n   670→\ts.current = &chunkedSeries{\n   671→\t\tChunkedSeries: prompb.ChunkedSeries{\n   672→\t\t\tLabels: res.ChunkedSeries[0].Labels,\n   673→\t\t\tChunks: res.ChunkedSeries[0].Chunks,\n   674→\t\t},\n   675→\t\tmint: s.mint,\n   676→\t\tmaxt: s.maxt,\n   677→\t}\n   678→\n   679→\treturn true\n   680→}\n   681→\n   682→func (s *chunkedSeriesSet) At() storage.Series {\n   683→\treturn s.current\n   684→}\n   685→\n   686→func (s *chunkedSeriesSet) Err() error {\n   687→\treturn s.err\n   688→}\n   689→\n   690→func (*chunkedSeriesSet) Warnings() annotations.Annotations {\n   691→\treturn nil\n   692→}\n   693→\n   694→type chunkedSeries struct {\n   695→\tprompb.ChunkedSeries\n   696→\tmint, maxt int64\n   697→}\n   698→\n   699→var _ storage.Series = &chunkedSeries{}\n   700→\n   701→func (s *chunkedSeries) Labels() labels.Labels {\n   702→\tb := labels.NewScratchBuilder(0)\n   703→\treturn s.ToLabels(&b, nil)\n   704→}\n   705→\n   706→func (s *chunkedSeries) Iterator(it chunkenc.Iterator) chunkenc.Iterator {\n   707→\tcsIt, ok := it.(*chunkedSeriesIterator)\n   708→\tif ok {\n   709→\t\tcsIt.reset(s.Chunks, s.mint, s.maxt)\n   710→\t\treturn csIt\n   711→\t}\n   712→\treturn newChunkedSeriesIterator(s.Chunks, s.mint, s.maxt)\n   713→}\n   714→\n   715→type chunkedSeriesIterator struct {\n   716→\tchunks     []prompb.Chunk\n   717→\tidx        int\n   718→\tcur        chunkenc.Iterator\n   719→\tvalType    chunkenc.ValueType\n   720→\tmint, maxt int64\n   721→\n   722→\terr error\n   723→}\n   724→\n   725→var _ chunkenc.Iterator = &chunkedSeriesIterator{}\n   726→\n   727→func newChunkedSeriesIterator(chunks []prompb.Chunk, mint, maxt int64) *chunkedSeriesIterator {\n   728→\tit := &chunkedSeriesIterator{}\n   729→\tit.reset(chunks, mint, maxt)\n   730→\treturn it\n   731→}\n   732→\n   733→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) Next() chunkenc.ValueType {\n   734→\tif it.err != nil {\n   735→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   736→\t}\n   737→\tif len(it.chunks) == 0 {\n   738→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   739→\t}\n   740→\n   741→\tfor it.valType = it.cur.Next(); it.valType != chunkenc.ValNone; it.valType = it.cur.Next() {\n   742→\t\tatT := it.AtT()\n   743→\t\tif atT > it.maxt {\n   744→\t\t\tit.chunks = nil // Exhaust this iterator so follow-up calls to Next or Seek return fast.\n   745→\t\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   746→\t\t}\n   747→\t\tif atT >= it.mint {\n   748→\t\t\treturn it.valType\n   749→\t\t}\n   750→\t}\n   751→\n   752→\tif it.idx >= len(it.chunks)-1 {\n   753→\t\tit.valType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   754→\t} else {\n   755→\t\tit.idx++\n   756→\t\tit.resetIterator()\n   757→\t\tit.valType = it.Next()\n   758→\t}\n   759→\n   760→\treturn it.valType\n   761→}\n   762→\n   763→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) Seek(t int64) chunkenc.ValueType {\n   764→\tif it.err != nil {\n   765→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   766→\t}\n   767→\tif len(it.chunks) == 0 {\n   768→\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   769→\t}\n   770→\n   771→\tstartIdx := it.idx\n   772→\tit.idx += sort.Search(len(it.chunks)-startIdx, func(i int) bool {\n   773→\t\treturn it.chunks[startIdx+i].MaxTimeMs >= t\n   774→\t})\n   775→\tif it.idx > startIdx {\n   776→\t\tit.resetIterator()\n   777→\t} else {\n   778→\t\tts := it.cur.AtT()\n   779→\t\tif ts >= t {\n   780→\t\t\treturn it.valType\n   781→\t\t}\n   782→\t}\n   783→\n   784→\tfor it.valType = it.cur.Next(); it.valType != chunkenc.ValNone; it.valType = it.cur.Next() {\n   785→\t\tts := it.cur.AtT()\n   786→\t\tif ts > it.maxt {\n   787→\t\t\tit.chunks = nil // Exhaust this iterator so follow-up calls to Next or Seek return fast.\n   788→\t\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n   789→\t\t}\n   790→\t\tif ts >= t && ts >= it.mint {\n   791→\t\t\treturn it.valType\n   792→\t\t}\n   793→\t}\n   794→\n   795→\tit.valType = chunkenc.ValNone\n   796→\treturn it.valType\n   797→}\n   798→\n   799→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) resetIterator() {\n   800→\tif it.idx < len(it.chunks) {\n   801→\t\tchunk := it.chunks[it.idx]\n   802→\n   803→\t\tdecodedChunk, err := chunkenc.FromData(chunkenc.Encoding(chunk.Type), chunk.Data)\n   804→\t\tif err != nil {\n   805→\t\t\tit.err = err\n   806→\t\t\treturn\n   807→\t\t}\n   808→\n   809→\t\tit.cur = decodedChunk.Iterator(nil)\n   810→\t} else {\n   811→\t\tit.cur = chunkenc.NewNopIterator()\n   812→\t}\n   813→}\n   814→\n   815→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) reset(chunks []prompb.Chunk, mint, maxt int64) {\n   816→\tit.chunks = chunks\n   817→\tit.mint = mint\n   818→\tit.maxt = maxt\n   819→\tit.idx = 0\n   820→\tif len(chunks) > 0 {\n   821→\t\tit.resetIterator()\n   822→\t}\n   823→}\n   824→\n   825→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) At() (ts int64, v float64) {\n   826→\treturn it.cur.At()\n   827→}\n   828→\n   829→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) AtHistogram(h *histogram.Histogram) (int64, *histogram.Histogram) {\n   830→\treturn it.cur.AtHistogram(h)\n   831→}\n   832→\n   833→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) AtFloatHistogram(fh *histogram.FloatHistogram) (int64, *histogram.FloatHistogram) {\n   834→\treturn it.cur.AtFloatHistogram(fh)\n   835→}\n   836→\n   837→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) AtT() int64 {\n   838→\treturn it.cur.AtT()\n   839→}\n   840→\n   841→// TODO(krajorama): test AtST once we have a chunk format that provides ST.\n   842→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) AtST() int64 {\n   843→\treturn it.cur.AtST()\n   844→}\n   845→\n   846→func (it *chunkedSeriesIterator) Err() error {\n   847→\treturn it.err\n   848→}\n   849→\n   850→// validateLabelsAndMetricName validates the label names/values and metric names returned from remote read,\n   851→// also making sure that there are no labels with duplicate names.\n   852→func validateLabelsAndMetricName(ls []prompb.Label) error {\n   853→\tfor i, l := range ls {\n   854→\t\tif l.Name == labels.MetricName && !model.UTF8Validation.IsValidMetricName(l.Value) {\n   855→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid metric name: %v\", l.Value)\n   856→\t\t}\n   857→\t\tif !model.UTF8Validation.IsValidLabelName(l.Name) {\n   858→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label name: %v\", l.Name)\n   859→\t\t}\n   860→\t\tif !model.LabelValue(l.Value).IsValid() {\n   861→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label value: %v\", l.Value)\n   862→\t\t}\n   863→\t\tif i > 0 && l.Name == ls[i-1].Name {\n   864→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"duplicate label with name: %v\", l.Name)\n   865→\t\t}\n   866→\t}\n   867→\treturn nil\n   868→}\n   869→\n   870→// ToLabelMatchers converts Prometheus label matchers to protobuf label matchers.\n   871→func ToLabelMatchers(matchers []*labels.Matcher) ([]*prompb.LabelMatcher, error) {\n   872→\tpbMatchers := make([]*prompb.LabelMatcher, 0, len(matchers))\n   873→\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n   874→\t\tvar mType prompb.LabelMatcher_Type\n   875→\t\tswitch m.Type {\n   876→\t\tcase labels.MatchEqual:\n   877→\t\t\tmType = prompb.LabelMatcher_EQ\n   878→\t\tcase labels.MatchNotEqual:\n   879→\t\t\tmType = prompb.LabelMatcher_NEQ\n   880→\t\tcase labels.MatchRegexp:\n   881→\t\t\tmType = prompb.LabelMatcher_RE\n   882→\t\tcase labels.MatchNotRegexp:\n   883→\t\t\tmType = prompb.LabelMatcher_NRE\n   884→\t\tdefault:\n   885→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"invalid matcher type\")\n   886→\t\t}\n   887→\t\tpbMatchers = append(pbMatchers, &prompb.LabelMatcher{\n   888→\t\t\tType:  mType,\n   889→\t\t\tName:  m.Name,\n   890→\t\t\tValue: m.Value,\n   891→\t\t})\n   892→\t}\n   893→\treturn pbMatchers, nil\n   894→}\n   895→\n   896→// FromLabelMatchers converts protobuf label matchers to Prometheus label matchers.\n   897→func FromLabelMatchers(matchers []*prompb.LabelMatcher) ([]*labels.Matcher, error) {\n   898→\tresult := make([]*labels.Matcher, 0, len(matchers))\n   899→\tfor _, matcher := range matchers {\n   900→\t\tvar mtype labels.MatchType\n   901→\t\tswitch matcher.Type {\n   902→\t\tcase prompb.LabelMatcher_EQ:\n   903→\t\t\tmtype = pool.\n\t\t\tmarshalPool.Put(&b)\n\t\t\tchks = chks[:0]\n\t\t\tframeBytesLeft = maxDataLength\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := iter.Err(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ss.Warnings(), err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn ss.Warnings(), ss.Err()\n}\n\n// MergeLabels merges two sets of sorted proto labels, preferring those in\n// primary to those in secondary when there is an overlap.\nfunc MergeLabels(primary, secondary []prompb.Label) []prompb.Label {\n\tresult := make([]prompb.Label, 0, len(primary)+len(secondary))\n\ti, j := 0, 0\n\tfor i < len(primary) && j < len(secondary) {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase primary[i].Name < secondary[j].Name:\n\t\t\tresult = append(result, primary[i])\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\tcase primary[i].Name > secondary[j].Name:\n\t\t\tresult = append(result, secondary[j])\n\t\t\tj++\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tresult = append(result, primary[i])\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t\tj++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor ; i < len(primary); i++ {\n\t\tresult = append(result, primary[i])\n\t}\n\tfor ; j < len(secondary); j++ {\n\t\tresult = append(result, secondary[j])\n\t}\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// errSeriesSet implements storage.SeriesSet, just returning an error.\ntype {\n\treturn e.err\n}\n\nfunc (errSeriesSet) Warnings() annotations.Annotations { return nil }\n\n// concreteSeriesSet implements storage.SeriesSet.\ntype concreteSeriesSet struct {\n\tcur {\n\treturn c.labels.Copy()\n}\n\nfunc (c *concreteSeries) Iterator(it chunkenc.Iterator) chunkenc.Iterator {\n\tif csi, ok := it.(*concreteSeriesIterator); ok {\n\t\tcsi.reset(c)\n\t\treturn csi\n\t}\n\treturn newConcreteSeriesIterator(c)\n}\n\n// concreteSeriesIterator implements storage.SeriesIterator.\ntype concreteSeriesIterator struct {\n\tfloatsCur     int\n\thistogramsCur ValFloatHistogram, respectively.\n\tcurH  *histogram.Histogram\n\tcurFH *histogram.FloatHistogram\n}\n\nfunc newConcreteSeriesIterator(series *concreteSeries) chunkenc.Iterator {\n\treturn &concreteSeriesIterator{\n\t\tfloatsCur:     -1,\n\t\thistogramsCur: -1,\n\t\tcurValType:    chunkenc.ValNone,\n\t\tseries:        series,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) reset(series *concreteSeries) {\n\tc.floatsCur = -1\n\tc.histogramsCur = -1\n\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n\tc.series = series\n\tc.err = nil\n}\n\n// Seek implements storage.SeriesIterator.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) Seek(t int64) chunkenc.ValueType {\n\tif c.err != nil {\n\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n\t}\n\tif c.floatsCur == -1 {\n\t\tc.floatsCur = 0\n\t}\n\tif c.histogramsCur == -1 {\n\t\tc.histogramsCur = 0\n\t}\n\tif c.floatsCur >= len(c.series.floats) && c.histogramsCur >= len(c.series.histograms) {\n\t\treturn chunkenc.ValNone\n\t}\n\n\t// No-op check.\n\tif (c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloat && c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp >= t) ||\n\t\t((c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram || c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram) && c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp >= t) {\n\t\treturn c.curValType\n\t}\n\n\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n\n\t// Binary search between current position and end for both float and histograms samples.\n\tc.floatsCur += sort.Search(len(c.series.floats)-c.floatsCur, func(n int) bool {\n\t\treturn c.series.floats[n+c.floatsCur].Timestamp >= t\n\t})\n\tc.histogramsCur += sort.Search(len(c.series.histograms)-c.histogramsCur, func(n int) bool {\n\t\treturn c.series.histograms[n+c.histogramsCur].Timestamp >= t\n\t})\n\tswitch {\n\tcase c.floatsCur < len(c.series.floats) && c.histogramsCur < len(c.series.histograms):\n\t\t// If float samples and histogram samples have overlapping timestamps prefer the float samples.\n\t\tif c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp <= c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp {\n\t\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n\t\t}\n\t\t// When the timestamps do not overlap the cursor for the non-selected sample type has advanced too\n\t\t// far; we decrement it back down here.\n\t\tif c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp != c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp {\n\t\t\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloat {\n\t\t\t\tc.histogramsCur--\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tc.floatsCur--\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase c.floatsCur < len(c.series.floats):\n\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloat\n\tcase c.histogramsCur < len(c.series.histograms):\n\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n\t}\n\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram {\n\t\tc.setCurrentHistogram()\n\t}\n\tif c.err != nil {\n\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValNone\n\t}\n\treturn c.curValType\n}\n\n// setCurrentHistogram pre-fills either the curH or the curFH field with a\n// converted model histogram and sets c.curValType accordingly. It validates the\n// histogram and sets c.err accordingly. This all has to be done in Seek() and\n// Next() already so that we know if the histogram we got from the remote-read\n// source is valid or not before we allow the AtHistogram()/AtFloatHistogram()\n// call.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) setCurrentHistogram() {\n\tpbH := c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur]\n\n\t// Basic schema check first.\n\tschema := pbH.Schema\n\tif !histogram.IsKnownSchema(schema) {\n\t\tc.err = histogram.UnknownSchemaError(schema)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif pbH.IsFloatHistogram() {\n\t\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram\n\t\tmFH := pbH.ToFloatHistogram()\n\t\tif mFH.Schema > histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax && mFH.Schema <= histogram.ExponentialSchemaMaxReserved {\n\t\t\t// This is a very slow path, but it should only happen if the\n\t\t\t// sample is from a newer Prometheus version that supports higher\n\t\t\t// resolution.\n\t\t\tif err := mFH.ReduceResolution(histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tc.err = err\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := mFH.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\t\tc.err = err\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.curFH = mFH\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tc.curValType = chunkenc.ValHistogram\n\tmH := pbH.ToIntHistogram()\n\tif mH.Schema > histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax && mH.Schema <= histogram.ExponentialSchemaMaxReserved {\n\t\t// This is a very slow path, but it should only happen if the\n\t\t// sample is from a newer Prometheus version that supports higher\n\t\t// resolution.\n\t\tif err := mH.ReduceResolution(histogram.ExponentialSchemaMax); err != nil {\n\t\t\tc.err = err\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif err := mH.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\tc.err = err\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tc.curH = mH\n}\n\n// At implements chunkenc.Iterator.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) At() (t int64, v float64) {\n\tif c.curValType != chunkenc.ValFloat {\n\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on a float sample\")\n\t}\n\ts := c.series.floats[c.floatsCur]\n\treturn s.Timestamp, s.Value\n}\n\n// AtHistogram implements chunkenc.Iterator.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtHistogram(*histogram.Histogram) (int64, *histogram.Histogram) {\n\tif c.curValType != chunkenc.ValHistogram {\n\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on an integer histogram sample\")\n\t}\n\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curH\n}\n\n// AtFloatHistogram implements chunkenc.Iterator.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtFloatHistogram(*histogram.FloatHistogram) (int64, *histogram.FloatHistogram) {\n\tswitch c.curValType {\n\tcase chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram:\n\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curFH\n\tcase chunkenc.ValHistogram:\n\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp, c.curH.ToFloat(nil)\n\tdefault:\n\t\tpanic(\"iterator is not on a histogram sample\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// AtT implements chunkenc.Iterator.\nfunc (c *concreteSeriesIterator) AtT() int64 {\n\tif c.curValType == chunkenc.ValHistogram || c.curValType == chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram {\n\t\treturn c.series.histograms[c.histogramsCur].Timestamp\n\t}\n\treturn c.series.floats[c.floatsCur].Timestamp\n}\n\n// TODO(krajorama): implement AtST. 152→\n   153→func (*MetricStreamingDecoder) GetLabel() {\n   154→\tpanic(\"don't use GetLabel, use Label instead\")\n   155→}\n   156→\n   157→// unsafeLabelAdder adds labels for a single metric.\n
